Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fragmetric began as **Solana’s first native liquid (re)staking protocol** and evolved into the advanced **FRAG-22 asset management standard**. This new standard seamlessly integrates multi-asset deposits, precise reward distribution, and modular yield sourcing, empowering both developers and users to efficiently access sophisticated DeFi strategies. Leveraging Solana’s Token extension, FRAG-22 provides transparent, real time reward tracking and superior liquidity management. With clearly defined operational roles and secure protocols, Fragmetric sets a benchmark for composability, scalability, and user experience within the Solana ecosystem. Fragmetric’s mission is to build a **secure**, **transparent**, and **highly efficient** asset management infrastructure that empowers users and enhances the stability of Solana’s financial and security ecosystem. **Stake Twice, Earn More.**

Website: [https://fragmetric.xyz](https://fragmetric.xyz/)
Discord: [https://discord.gg/fragmetric](https://discord.gg/fragmetric)
Twitter: [https://x.com/fragmetric](https://x.com/fragmetric)

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome#quick-links)

fragAsset

FRAG²

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

Turn Your FRAG into FRAG² and Be Part of Fragmetric’s Next Chapter. By staking and holding, you write yourself into our shared history.

*   **Built by Believers:** Staking FRAG into FRAG² unites you with a community shaping Fragmetric’s vision and driving collective growth.
*   **Fragmetric Vote Token:** FRAG² holders receive Fragmetric Vote Tokens (FVT) to propose initiatives, vote on decisions, and lead community governance.
*   **Earn More with FRAG²:** Stake FRAG to earn FRAG APY and boost your F Points, rewarding your active commitment to Fragmetric.

[fragBTC](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc)

Navigation

fragAsset

fragJTO

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

fragJTO is the first non-SOL Liquid Restaking Token (LRT) introduced by Fragmetric. By staking JTO, the governance token of the Jito Protocol, you receive fragJTO, which represents your staked JTO and entitles you to:

*   **MEV Rewards:** Your JTO is utilized to secure TipRouter, a core component of the MEV ecosystem on Solana. The MEV tips generated here are shared with fragJTO holders, enhancing overall APY.
*   **Additional Restaking Revenue:** With integrations on the Jito (Re)staking Protocol, including collaborations with NCNs, Fragmetric efficiently redistributes extra restaking rewards to fragJTO holders.

> Rewards within the protocol are distributed in two ways: when Jito (Re)staking rewards arrive in JTO that can be deposited back into fragJTO, the protocol uses auto-compounding to grow fragJTO’s APY. If the rewards are paid in tokens not supported by the protocol, users can manually claim those tokens at any time. This dual model maximizes yields for fragJTO while ensuring users maintain direct control over any non-compounding rewards.

[fragSOL](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[fragBTC](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc)

fragAsset

fragSOL

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

fragSOL is Solana’s first Liquid Restaking Token (LRT) and the culmination of Fragmetric’s technological innovation. By restaking SOL or other Liquid Staking Tokens (JitoSOL, mSOL, BNSOL, or bbSOL) through the Fragmetric protocol, you receive fragSOL, which represents your restaked SOL or LST and entitles you to:

*   **Solana Staking Yield:** Fragmetric collaborates with top-tier yield-focused protocols, aiming to deliver competitive returns to fragSOL holders.
*   **MEV Rewards:** All SOL and LSTs deposited into Fragmetric are used to secure TipRouter, the first Node Consensus Network (NCN) under Jito Restaking. MEV tips generated from these activities are distributed to fragSOL holders, boosting overall APY.
*   **Additional Restaking Revenue:** With integrations on the Jito (Re)staking Protocol, including collaborations with NCNs, Fragmetric efficiently redistributes extra restaking rewards to fragSOL holders.

Rewards within the protocol are distributed in two ways:

*   When NCN/AVS rewards are distributed in tokens that can be deposited back into fragSOL, the protocol uses auto-compounding to increase fragSOL’s APY.
*   If the rewards are paid in tokens not supported for deposit, users can manually claim those tokens at any time. This dual approach ensures the best possible yield for fragSOL while giving users direct control over any non-compounding rewards.

[fragJTO](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragjto)

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

fragAsset

fragBTC

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [How fragBTC Works](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc#how-fragbtc-works)
    
*   [Why fragBTC Matters for Bitcoin Holders and Solana](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc#why-fragbtc-matters-for-bitcoin-holders-and-solana)
    

fragBTC is the first yield-bearing Bitcoin, co-launched by Fragmetric, Solv Protocol, and Zeus Network. By staking BTC-pegged assets, you receive fragBTC, which offers a compelling opportunity to earn sustainable yields while contributing to Solana’s DeFi growth.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc#how-fragbtc-works)

How fragBTC Works

fragBTC generates its base yield through SolvBTC.JUP, a BTC yield strategy built by Solv Protocol. This strategy sources BTC-denominated returns by providing liquidity to the Jupiter Liquidity Provider (JLP) Pool on Jupiter Exchange. To reduce exposure to market volatility, SolvBTC.JUP applies a delta-neutral approach, offering risk-adjusted yield profiles designed to accommodate varying levels of risk tolerance among Bitcoin holders. fragBTC starts with SolvBTC.JUP and will expand to a variety of BTCFi strategies, allowing users to stake their Bitcoin-pegged assets on Solana while maintaining liquidity and earning yields.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragbtc#why-fragbtc-matters-for-bitcoin-holders-and-solana)

Why fragBTC Matters for Bitcoin Holders and Solana

FragBTC marks a pioneering effort at the intersection of Bitcoin and the Solana ecosystem.

*   For Bitcoin holders, it unlocks a reliable avenue to earn yield while preserving both BTC exposure and on-chain liquidity — tackling the long-standing inefficiency of idle Bitcoin capital.
*   For the Solana network, fragBTC introduces deep Bitcoin liquidity that enhances overall capital efficiency.

By combining this sustainable yield-generating model with Solana’s fast transactions and low fees, fragBTC is positioned to solve the long-standing issue of over $1 trillion in idle BTC capital.

[fragJTO](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragjto)
[FRAG²](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/frag2)

Wrapped fragAsset

wfragSOL

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

wfragSOL is wrapped versions of fragSOL, designed for broader DeFi compatibility. Some DeFi protocols do not support Token Extension (also known as Token-2022), an advanced token program on the Solana blockchain. To address this, wfragSOL is created as DeFi-compatible version of fragSOL, with the wrapped tokens pegged to its respective token.

[FRAG²](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/frag2)
[wfragJTO](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/wfragjto)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Wrapped fragAsset

wfragJTO

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

wfragJTO is wrapped versions of fragJTO, designed for broader DeFi compatibility. Some DeFi protocols do not support Token Extension (also known as Token-2022), an advanced token program on the Solana blockchain. To address this, wfragJTO is created as DeFi-compatible version of fragJTO, with the wrapped tokens pegged to its respective token.[](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/wfragsol/)

[wfragSOL](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/wfragsol)
[wfragBTC](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/wfragbtc)

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs#upgrade-authority-owner)

Upgrade Authority Owner
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs#multisig-committees)

Multisig Committees

Fragmetric’s deployed programs are designed to be upgradeable for several key reasons. First, as the protocol is rolled out in multiple phases, program upgrades are necessary to enable careful adjustments to core protocol parameters. Second, upgradability ensures that the team can respond swiftly in case of emergencies, maintaining the security and stability of the platform. All deployed programs within Fragmetric are governed by a multisig, managed by multiple core contributors. As the protocol evolves, the multisig governance structure will gradually expand to include members of the broader Fragmetric ecosystem, further enhancing decentralization. Fragmetric uses Squads v4, Solana’s leading multisig infrastructure. This system has undergone multiple security audits, and Squads Protocol v4 has successfully completed two formal verifications, ensuring its robustness and reliability.

[Release Notes](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes)

DeFi Integration

3\. DeFi Metadata

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Integration Requirements](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#integration-requirements)
    
*   [Options for Integration](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#options-for-integration)
    
*   [1\. Provide a Custom API Endpoint](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#1-provide-a-custom-api-endpoint)
    
*   [2\. Provide an Integration Guide](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#2-provide-an-integration-guide)
    

To provide visibility into your pool’s status within the Fragmetric platform, you must supply metadata about your DeFi pool, including **TVL** and **APY**. This data will be shown on the Fragmetric app alongside F Point information to give users a clear view of where their funds are deployed and how they’re performing.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#integration-requirements)

Integration Requirements
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "apy": 0.4655,
      "tvl": "1234000000000"
    }
    

*   `apy`: Annual percentage yield, as a decimal. (e.g., 0.4655 = 46.55%)
*   `tvl`: Total value locked in the pool. The unit can be: USD, SOL or the relevant wfragAsset. (e.g., wfragSOL, wfragBTC, etc.)

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#options-for-integration)

Options for Integration
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#1-provide-a-custom-api-endpoint)

1\. Provide a Custom API Endpoint

You may expose a minimal REST API returning the structure above. We’ll consume this endpoint periodically and associate it with your pool based on a consistent `pool address`.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata#2-provide-an-integration-guide)

2\. Provide an Integration Guide

If you already publish TVL and APY via your own analytics API or frontend, simply share:

*   The public URL or API.
*   How to derive tvl and apy values for your pool.
*   How to match your internal pool identifier with the pool address used in our system.

We do not require you to build a new API. We only need a **reliable way to extract the data**, aligned with the same `pool address` used for F Point snapshotting.

[2\. F Point Snapshot](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot)
[4\. Rewards Distribution](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution)

Fragmetric SDK is the official TypeScript/JavaScript client for interacting with Fragmetric Solana programs. It supports both browser apps and Node.js environments, and includes a CLI for operational workflows and hardware wallet support.

The Fragmetric Snapshot package enables transparent tracking of DeFi participants’ shares. Fragmetric’s internal scheduler uses this package to regularly capture the current status of users’ DeFi participation.

restaking@0.5.0

Solana Mainnet

February 17, 2025

Liquid Restaking Program v0.5.0 Released
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#restaking-protocol-integration)

Restaking Protocol Integration

*   Jito Restaking Vault Program.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#staking-protocol-integration)

Staking Protocol Integration
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   SPL Stake Pool Program.
*   Marinade Stake Pool Program.
*   Sanctum Single Validator SPL Stake Pool Program.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#fund-implementation)

Fund Implementation

*   Fund Operator:
    *   A finite state machine which fully circulates underlying assets with different types of assets, such as SOL, LSTs, nSOL and VRT based on the fund strategy and withdrawal requests.
    *   A single type of instruction can be called repeatedly to cycle through entire asset flows, regardless of each state.
    *   Anyone can call this operator to execute asset flows, though authorization is required to configure the fund strategy.
*   Restaking Rewards Compounding:
    *   The first restaking rewards, JitoSOL, from TipRouter is being compounded into each funds (fragSOL, fragJTO).
*   De-Fi Integration Support:
    *   Wrap & Unwrap instructions have been released.
    *   LRT (SPL Token 2022) can be wrapped into legacy SPL Token to facilitate De-Fi protocol integration.
    *   Wrapped token can be utilized in various De-Fi protocols.
    *   Still, restaking rewards shall be distributed with transparency.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#fund-configuration)

Fund Configuration

*   fragSOL
    *   Withdrawal and transfer enabled.
*   fragJTO
    *   A new fund accepting JTO released.
    *   Withdrawal and transfer enabled.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#audit-reports)

Audit Reports

*   [QuantStamp](https://fragmetric-assets.s3.ap-northeast-2.amazonaws.com/audit-25-02-quantstamp.pdf)
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#restaking%400-2-3)

restaking@0.2.3

Solana Mainnet

October 18, 2024

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#liquid-restaking-program-v0-2-3-released)

Liquid Restaking Program v0.2.3 Released
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#fund-implementation-2)

Fund Implementation

*   Deposit & Mint:
    *   Native SOL deposits to the Fund and mint LRT.
    *   LST deposits to the Fund and mint LRT. - Deposits using liquid staking tokens (LSTs), including mSOL, bSOL, and jitoSOL.
*   LST Pricing:
    *   Pricing based on stake pools ensures accurate valuation of deposits using LSTs, reflecting real-time stake pool data for tokens like mSOL, bSOL, and jitoSOL.
*   Withdrawal & Burn:
    *   Native SOL withdrawal from the LRT Fund and burn LRT. Withdrawal and burn ratio is based on LRT pricing at withdrawal.
*   Fund Operator Implementation:
    *   Operator Instructions:
        *   Withdrawal batch process invocation.
        *   Reward pool update to calculate contribution.
*   Reward System Implementation:
    *   Implementation of reward accrual, tracking, and settlement covering various reward types, including arbitrary tokens, points, and SOL.
    *   Tracking every LRT transfer across the entire Solana network and calculating contributions for rewards using the Token Extension (Token2022 program) - Transfer Hook.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#fund-configuration-2)

Fund Configuration

*   Currently supports SOL, mSOL, and jitoSOL deposits, depending on their respective capacities.
*   Withdrawal and transfer will be enabled with upcoming update on the Mainnet.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#reward-system-configuration)

Reward System Configuration

*   Base Pool (POOL\_ID: 0) : Reward pool for future AVS/NCN rewards.
*   Bonus Pool (POOL\_ID: 1) : Reward pool for Fragmetric’s own rewards including fPoint, etc.
*   F Point (REWARD\_ID: 0): Points for Fragmetric’s future token airdrops.
*   Customized Accrual Rate: A contribution boost is applied only to the Bonus Pool and is effective only for fPoint rewards. It is effective when deposits are made using the Backpack wallet.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes#audit-reports-2)

Audit Reports

*   [Certora](https://fragmetric-assets.s3.ap-northeast-2.amazonaws.com/audit-24-10-certora.pdf)

DeFi Integration

5\. Caution for Deposit Instruction

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [What Are Pricing Source Accounts?](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#what-are-pricing-source-accounts%3F)
    
*   [Ground Rules for Required Accounts](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#ground-rules-for-required-accounts)
    
*   [How to Include These Accounts](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#how-to-include-these-accounts)
    
*   [1\. Use the SDK to build an instruction](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#1-use-the-sdk-to-build-an-instruction)
    
*   [2\. Read the addresses from the fund account](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#2-read-the-addresses-from-the-fund-account)
    

If your protocol integrates Fragmetric’s deposit logic by manually constructing and including an instruction either:

*   `user_deposit_sol`
*   `user_deposit_supported_token`

..you must ensure that **all required pricing source accounts** are included in the transaction. These accounts are **not declared in the IDL** and must be resolved explicitly — either manually, via SDK, or by reading the fund account data.

Do not hardcode account lists. Do not assume the current set of accounts will remain valid after governance updates (e.g. adding supported tokens or vaults).

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#what-are-pricing-source-accounts%3F)

What Are Pricing Source Accounts?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These accounts are used to price deposits and determine how much fragAsset should be minted. They are derived from the **dynamic configuration of the fund**, and may vary over time or between assets (e.g., `fragSOL`, `fragJTO`, `fragBTC`).

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#ground-rules-for-required-accounts)

Ground Rules for Required Accounts

For every `fragAsset` fund, you must include accounts of:

*   `fund.supported_tokens[0:fund.num_supported_tokens].pricing_source.address`
*   `fund.restaking_vaults[0:fund.num_restaking_vaults].pricing_source.address`
*   `fund.normalized_token.pricing_source.address` — only if `fund.normalized_token.enabled == 1`

Some accounts may appear multiple times (especially in `fragBTC`, which consists of pegged assets). You can manually deduplicate these accounts when building your transaction.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#how-to-include-these-accounts)

How to Include These Accounts
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can derive this list by reading the on-chain fund account data for each `fragAsset`, following the rules above. Also there are two safe, forward-compatible options to resolve these accounts:

*   **Use the SDK**: The `@fragmetric-labs/sdk` will resolve all required pricing source accounts for you based on the latest fund state.
*   **Read the fund account**: Each fund account data includes the list of pricing source addresses. Use this list to avoid manually deriving the accounts in your transaction.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#1-use-the-sdk-to-build-an-instruction)

1\. Use the SDK to build an instruction

You can build a full deposit transaction. And if you need unsigned transaction or just a part of the instructions. you can just build a blueprint transaction without serialize it. Check [Tools > Fragmetric SDK (offchain) > Deposit](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/sdk/offchain/quickstart#3-deposit)
 for details.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/deposit-instruction#2-read-the-addresses-from-the-fund-account)

2\. Read the addresses from the fund account

You can read addresses directly from the fund account before build a deposit instruction to include all required pricing sources. There are below fields containing pricing source account information in the **fund account** data like below:

Copy

Ask AI

    /// ... starts from data offset: 0x9000 (36864)
    num_pricing_source_addresses: u8,
    pricing_source_addresses: [Pubkey; 33],
    

Check [Developers > Solana Programs](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs#fragmetric-liquid-restaking-program)
 for the address of fund accounts.

[4\. Rewards Distribution](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution)
[Fragmetric CLI](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Fragmetric Docs

[Fragmetric Docs home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_light_2.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_dark_2.svg)](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/)

Navigation

DeFi Integration

Overview

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Table of Contents](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#table-of-contents)
    
*   [1\. Integration Status](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#1-integration-status)
    
*   [2\. FPoint Snapshot](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#2-fpoint-snapshot)
    
*   [3\. Metadata Integration](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#3-metadata-integration)
    
*   [4\. Rewards Distribution](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#4-rewards-distribution)
    
*   [5\. Caution for Deposit Instruction](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#5-caution-for-deposit-instruction)
    

This documentation provides integration guidelines for DeFi protocols connecting to the Fragmetric ecosystem. Fragmetric supports a wide range of strategy types including **liquidity, looping, yield trading, lending, and bridging**. Each integrated DeFi pool is characterized by:

*   a pool address — uniquely identifying the DeFi strategy instance,
*   a receipt token mint — fragSOL, fragJTO, or fragBTC, denoting the underlying asset class being restaked,
*   and (for liquidity protocols) a paired token used within the DeFi pool.

DeFi integrations revolve around **wfragSOL, wfragJTO, wfragBTC**, etc. These are wrapped versions of Fragmetric’s restaking receipt tokens. Since fragSOL, fragJTO, and fragBTC are Token-2022 tokens (offering features like transfer hooks and metadata), they are not natively compatible with many existing DeFi protocols. To solve this, Fragmetric provides legacy SPL-compatible wrapped tokens under the legacy token program. These wfragAsset tokens mirror the balance and behavior of their token2022 counterparts but offer seamless composability across standard SPL DeFi systems.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#table-of-contents)

Table of Contents
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#1-integration-status)

1\. Integration Status

A list of supported DeFi pools, including their pool address, receipt token category, and integration progress.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#2-fpoint-snapshot)

2\. FPoint Snapshot

Explains how DeFi participants become eligible for FPoints, how partners should integrate snapshot logic, and how to surface user accruals in their app.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#3-metadata-integration)

3\. Metadata Integration

Instructions for exposing APY, TVL, and other pool metrics via REST API for Fragmetric frontend consumption.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#4-rewards-distribution)

4\. Rewards Distribution

Describes the reward claiming model where DeFi pool admins receive and redistribute aggregated rewards on behalf of their participants.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/overview#5-caution-for-deposit-instruction)

5\. Caution for Deposit Instruction

Technical notes for protocols that integrate Fragmetric’s deposit instruction into their custom transactions. This includes guidance on resolving non-IDL pricing source accounts, which are required for accurate pricing and may change dynamically if the fund updates supported tokens.

[Release Notes](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/release-notes)
[1\. Integration Status](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/integration-status)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Navigation

DeFi Integration

2\. F Point Snapshot

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Integration Requirements](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#integration-requirements)
    
*   [Snapshot Rules](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#snapshot-rules)
    
*   [To Display User F Point Accrual from Your Pool](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#to-display-user-f-point-accrual-from-your-pool)
    

**F Point** is a unified point system used to measure user contributions across DeFi integrations and Fragmetric platform. It is used to determine future eligibility for the `FRAG` token airdrop. To support this, Fragmetric takes periodic snapshots of `wfragAsset` balances held within integrated DeFi protocols. Each DeFi partner is responsible for implementing a snapshot module that emits per-user balance data in a standardized format.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#integration-requirements)

Integration Requirements
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must implement a `SourceStreamFactory` that produces `{ owner, baseTokenBalance }` entries for all users in your protocol’s pool.

*   Create your snapshot source module under: [https://github.com/fragmetric-labs/fragmetric-snapshot/tree/main/src/commands/snapshot/source](https://github.com/fragmetric-labs/fragmetric-snapshot/tree/main/src/commands/snapshot/source)
    
*   Implement the snapshot logic:
    *   Validate arguments.
    *   Call `produceSnapshot(...)` for each user.
    *   Call `close(...)` at the end or on error.
*   Register your source in `sources.ts`.
*   Implement a smoke test file for the actual pool with your source.
*   Submit a pull request.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#snapshot-rules)

Snapshot Rules
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  TVL Must Match The total of all baseTokenBalance values must exactly equal the pool’s actual `wfragAsset` TVL. This guarantees snapshot integrity and fair accounting.
2.  Liquidity Category Exception For protocols in the **LIQUIDITY** category, You may convert the full LP token value into synthetic `wfragAsset` terms (e.g., `fragSOL + JitoSOL → wfragSOL`). This is allowed to compensate liquidity providers for impermanent loss and to incentivize liquidity depth in DeFi integrations.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/fpoint-snapshot#to-display-user-f-point-accrual-from-your-pool)

To Display User F Point Accrual from Your Pool
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To show users their current F Point accruals from your DeFi pool, utilize the following public API: [https://api.fragmetric.xyz/v1/#/operations/GetUserFPointEstimationsByDeFiPool](https://api.fragmetric.xyz/v1/#/operations/GetUserFPointEstimationsByDeFiPool)
 You can pass the user’s wallet address and your pool address as parameters. The response provides real-time accrual data, which can be rendered in your frontend to reflect live F Point estimates. Use this API to integrate user-facing F Point display into your app or dashboard.

[1\. Integration Status](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/integration-status)
[3\. DeFi Metadata](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/defi-metadata)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Development

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Custom Ports](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#custom-ports)
    
*   [Mintlify Versions](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#mintlify-versions)
    
*   [Validating Links](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#validating-links)
    
*   [Deployment](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#deployment)
    
*   [Code Formatting](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#code-formatting)

**Prerequisite**: Please install Node.js (version 19 or higher) before proceeding.  
Please upgrade to `docs.json` before proceeding and delete the legacy `mint.json` file.

Follow these steps to install and run Mintlify on your operating system: **Step 1**: Install Mintlify:

npm

yarn

Copy

Ask AI

    npm i -g mintlify
    

**Step 2**: Navigate to the docs directory (where the `docs.json` file is located) and execute the following command:

Copy

Ask AI

    mintlify dev
    

A local preview of your documentation will be available at `http://localhost:3000`.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#custom-ports)

Custom Ports

By default, Mintlify uses port 3000. You can customize the port Mintlify runs on by using the `--port` flag. To run Mintlify on port 3333, for instance, use this command:

Copy

Ask AI

    mintlify dev --port 3333
    

If you attempt to run Mintlify on a port that’s already in use, it will use the next available port:

Copy

Ask AI

    Port 3000 is already in use. Trying 3001 instead.
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#mintlify-versions)

Mintlify Versions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please note that each CLI release is associated with a specific version of Mintlify. If your local website doesn’t align with the production version, please update the CLI:

npm

yarn

Copy

Ask AI

    npm i -g mintlify@latest
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#validating-links)

Validating Links
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The CLI can assist with validating reference links made in your documentation. To identify any broken links, use the following command:

Copy

Ask AI

    mintlify broken-links
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#deployment)

Deployment
---------------------------------------------------------------------

Unlimited editors available under the [Pro Plan](https://mintlify.com/pricing)
 and above.

If the deployment is successful, you should see the following:

![](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/images/checks-passed.png)

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#code-formatting)

Code Formatting
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We suggest using extensions on your IDE to recognize and format MDX. If you’re a VSCode user, consider the [MDX VSCode extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=unifiedjs.vscode-mdx)
 for syntax highlighting, and [Prettier](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=esbenp.prettier-vscode)
 for code formatting.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/development#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Error: Could not load the "sharp" module using the darwin-arm64 runtime

This may be due to an outdated version of node. Try the following:

1.  Remove the currently-installed version of mintlify: `npm remove -g mintlify`
2.  Upgrade to Node v19 or higher.
3.  Reinstall mintlify: `npm install -g mintlify`

Issue: Encountering an unknown error

Solution: Go to the root of your device and delete the ~/.mintlify folder. Afterwards, run `mintlify dev` again.

Curious about what changed in the CLI version? [Check out the CLI changelog.](https://www.npmjs.com/package/mintlify?activeTab=versions)

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Markdown Syntax

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Titles](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#titles)
    
*   [Subtitles](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#subtitles)
    
*   [Text Formatting](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#text-formatting)
    
*   [Linking to Pages](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#linking-to-pages)
    
*   [Blockquotes](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#blockquotes)
    
*   [Singleline](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#singleline)
    
*   [Multiline](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#multiline)
    
*   [LaTeX](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#latex)
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#titles)

Titles
---------------------------------------------------------------------

Best used for section headers.

Copy

Ask AI

    ## Titles
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#subtitles)

Subtitles

Best use to subsection headers.

Copy

Ask AI

    ### Subtitles
    

Each **title** and **subtitle** creates an anchor and also shows up on the table of contents on the right.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#text-formatting)

Text Formatting
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We support most markdown formatting. Simply add `**`, `_`, or `~` around text to format it.

| Style | How to write it | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Bold | `**bold**` | **bold** |
| Italic | `_italic_` | _italic_ |
| Strikethrough | `~strikethrough~` | ~strikethrough~ |

You can combine these. For example, write `**_bold and italic_**` to get _**bold and italic**_ text. You need to use HTML to write superscript and subscript text. That is, add `<sup>` or `<sub>` around your text.

| Text Size | How to write it | Result |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Superscript | `<sup>superscript</sup>` | superscript |
| Subscript | `<sub>subscript</sub>` | subscript |

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#linking-to-pages)

Linking to Pages
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add a link by wrapping text in `[]()`. You would write `[link to google](https://google.com)` to [link to google](https://google.com/)
. Links to pages in your docs need to be root-relative. Basically, you should include the entire folder path. For example, `[link to text](/writing-content/text)` links to the page “Text” in our components section. Relative links like `[link to text](../text)` will open slower because we cannot optimize them as easily.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#blockquotes)

Blockquotes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#singleline)

Singleline

To create a blockquote, add a `>` in front of a paragraph.

> Dorothy followed her through many of the beautiful rooms in her castle.

Copy

Ask AI

    > Dorothy followed her through many of the beautiful rooms in her castle.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#multiline)

Multiline

> Dorothy followed her through many of the beautiful rooms in her castle. The Witch bade her clean the pots and kettles and sweep the floor and keep the fire fed with wood.

Copy

Ask AI

    > Dorothy followed her through many of the beautiful rooms in her castle.
    >
    > The Witch bade her clean the pots and kettles and sweep the floor and keep the fire fed with wood.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/markdown#latex)

LaTeX

Mintlify supports [LaTeX](https://www.latex-project.org/)
 through the Latex component. 8 x (vk x H1 - H2) = (0,1)

Copy

Ask AI

    <Latex>8 x (vk x H1 - H2) = (0,1)</Latex>

| [SOON (wfragSOL)](https://www.usenexus.org/?origin=solanamainnet&destination=soon&token=22z73A4E7QjwjTsHGJptnALgBGuovEabCcQtPdBaQPpJ) | `PMST7CMBeJubWwhieuTvjgyEEwH8FLdNorZdvMJ3aVA` | [`PMST7CMBeJubWwhieuTvjgyEEwH8FLdNorZdvMJ3aVA`](https://explorer.solana.com/address/PMST7CMBeJubWwhieuTvjgyEEwH8FLdNorZdvMJ3aVA) | \-  |

[Fragmetric Docs home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_light_2.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_dark_2.svg)](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/)

Navigation

Navigation

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Navigation syntax](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#navigation-syntax)
    
*   [Folders](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#folders)
    
*   [Hidden Pages](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#hidden-pages)
    

The navigation menu is the list of links on every website. You will likely update `docs.json` every time you add a new page. Pages do not show up automatically.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#navigation-syntax)

Navigation syntax
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our navigation syntax is recursive which means you can make nested navigation groups. You don’t need to include `.mdx` in page names.

Regular Navigation

Nested Navigation

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "tabs": [\
        {\
          "tab": "Docs",\
          "groups": [\
            {\
              "group": "Getting Started",\
              "pages": ["quickstart"]\
            }\
          ]\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#folders)

Folders
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Simply put your MDX files in folders and update the paths in `docs.json`. For example, to have a page at `https://yoursite.com/your-folder/your-page` you would make a folder called `your-folder` containing an MDX file called `your-page.mdx`.

You cannot use `api` for the name of a folder unless you nest it inside another folder. Mintlify uses Next.js which reserves the top-level `api` folder for internal server calls. A folder name such as `api-reference` would be accepted.

Navigation With Folder

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "tabs": [\
        {\
          "tab": "Docs",\
          "groups": [\
            {\
              "group": "Group Name",\
              "pages": ["your-folder/your-page"]\
            }\
          ]\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/navigation#hidden-pages)

Hidden Pages
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

MDX files not included in `docs.json` will not show up in the sidebar but are accessible through the search bar and by linking directly to them.

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Basic
---------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/code#inline-code)

Inline Code

To denote a `word` or `phrase` as code, enclose it in backticks (\`).

Copy

Ask AI

    To denote a `word` or `phrase` as code, enclose it in backticks (`).
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/code#code-block)

Code Block

Use [fenced code blocks](https://www.markdownguide.org/extended-syntax/#fenced-code-blocks)
 by enclosing code in three backticks and follow the leading ticks with the programming language of your snippet to get syntax highlighting. Optionally, you can also write the name of your code after the programming language.

HelloWorld.java

Copy

Ask AI

    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```java HelloWorld.java
    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    ```

Navigation

Reusable Snippets

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Creating a custom snippet](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#creating-a-custom-snippet)
    
*   [Default export](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#default-export)
    
*   [Reusable variables](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#reusable-variables)
    
*   [Reusable components](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#reusable-components)
    

One of the core principles of software development is DRY (Don’t Repeat Yourself). This is a principle that apply to documentation as well. If you find yourself repeating the same content in multiple places, you should consider creating a custom snippet to keep your content in sync.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#creating-a-custom-snippet)

Creating a custom snippet
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Pre-condition**: You must create your snippet file in the `snippets` directory.

Any page in the `snippets` directory will be treated as a snippet and will not be rendered into a standalone page. If you want to create a standalone page from the snippet, import the snippet into another file and call it as a component.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#default-export)

Default export

1.  Add content to your snippet file that you want to re-use across multiple locations. Optionally, you can add variables that can be filled in via props when you import the snippet.

snippets/my-snippet.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    Hello world! This is my content I want to reuse across pages. My keyword of the
    day is {word}.
    

The content that you want to reuse must be inside the `snippets` directory in order for the import to work.

2.  Import the snippet into your destination file.

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import MySnippet from '/snippets/path/to/my-snippet.mdx';
    
    ## Header
    
    Lorem impsum dolor sit amet.
    
    <MySnippet word="bananas" />
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#reusable-variables)

Reusable variables

1.  Export a variable from your snippet file:

snippets/path/to/custom-variables.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    export const myName = 'my name';
    
    export const myObject = { fruit: 'strawberries' };
    

2.  Import the snippet from your destination file and use the variable:

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import { myName, myObject } from '/snippets/path/to/custom-variables.mdx';
    
    Hello, my name is {myName} and I like {myObject.fruit}.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/reusable-snippets#reusable-components)

Reusable components

1.  Inside your snippet file, create a component that takes in props by exporting your component in the form of an arrow function.

snippets/custom-component.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    export const MyComponent = ({ title }) => (
      <div>
        <h1>{title}</h1>
        <p>... snippet content ...</p>
      </div>
    );
    

MDX does not compile inside the body of an arrow function. Stick to HTML syntax when you can or use a default export if you need to use MDX.

2.  Import the snippet into your destination file and pass in the props

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import { MyComponent } from '/snippets/custom-component.mdx';
    
    Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet.
    
    <MyComponent title={'Custom title'} />
    

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

Tools

Fragmetric CLI

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)

On this page

*   [Requirements](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli#requirements)
    
*   [Quick Start](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli#quick-start)
    
*   [Deposit Example](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli#deposit-example)
    

Fragmetric SDK is the official TypeScript/JavaScript client for interacting with Fragmetric Solana programs. It supports browser apps, Node.js environments, and includes a CLI for operational workflow and hardware wallet support.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli#requirements)

Requirements

*   node >= 20

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/cli#quick-start)

Quick Start

Copy

Ask AI

    $ pnpx @fragmetric-labs/sdk@latest connect --help
    
    Usage: fragmetric connect [options]
    
    Create a REPL to interact with programs.
    
    Options:
      -e, --eval <EXPRESSION>       Evaluate an expression and quit.
      -h, --help                    display help for command
    
    Global Options:
      -V, --version                 output the version number
      -u, --url <URL_OR_MONIKER>    RPC URL or shorthand: [mainnet, devnet, testnet, local] (default: "mainnet")
      --ws <URL>                    Custom WebSocket RPC URL (overrides derived one)
      -c, --cluster <CLUSTER>       Program environment when using custom RPC URL (overrides derived one): [mainnet, devnet, testnet, local]
      -k, --keypairs <KEYPAIRS...>  One or more keypairs to automatically use as signers for transactions. First keypair will be used as feePayer. Accepts: JSON file
                                    path, directory of keypairs, base58/JSON literal, or literal for hardware wallets: [ledger].
      --format <FORMAT>             Set output format for evaluation: [pretty, json] (default: "pretty")
      --inspection <BOOL>           Set verbose logs in default transaction hooks: [true, false] (default: cluster != "mainnet")
    

The CLI has exactly same interface with the offchain SDK. Refer to [the SDK guide](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/tools/sdk/offchain/quickstart)
 for details.

[Fragmetric Docs home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_light_2.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/fragmetriclabs/logo/docs_title_dark_2.svg)](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/)

Navigation

DeFi Integration

4\. Rewards Distribution

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Process](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#process)
    
*   [1\. Register Token Account](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#1-register-token-account)
    
*   [2\. Delegate Reward Account](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#2-delegate-reward-account)
    
*   [3\. Track Token Accounts](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#3-track-token-accounts)
    
*   [4\. Claim and Distribute Rewards](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#4-claim-and-distribute-rewards)
    
*   [Claim Instruction](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#claim-instruction)
    
*   [Claim via SDK](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#claim-via-sdk)
    

We’ve been testing various models for distribution of rewards to DeFi pools. This policy is still under discussion and may change without notice until finalized.

Be noted that holding pure `fragAsset` ensures that the owner can claim rewards directly by executing a transaction. This guide is for handling rewards accrued from `wfragAsset`.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#process)

Process
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By design, Fragmetric’s restaking protocol tracks fragAsset (Token-2022) balances fully and accurately on-chain to account for each user’s portion of rewards. However, `wfragAsset` is a legacy SPL token and does not support the same tracking capabilities. Fragmetric uses the following approach for tracking `wfragAsset` contributions:

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#1-register-token-account)

1\. Register Token Account

Register specific `wfragAsset` **token accounts** to be tracked on-chain. A dedicated **reward account** is created per registered token account.

*   **wfragAsset Holder**: An alias for token accounts owned by a DeFi protocol that hold user `wfragAsset` deposits.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#2-delegate-reward-account)

2\. Delegate Reward Account

Initially, the created reward accounts belong to the Fragmetric Fund Manager (governance). The **authority to claim rewards** will be transferred to the appropriate governance address of the DeFi protocol.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#3-track-token-accounts)

3\. Track Token Accounts

Fund operations — which are executed regularly for each fund (`fragSOL`, `fragJTO`, `fragBTC`) — will track registered token accounts and update their contribution share in the reward system.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#4-claim-and-distribute-rewards)

4\. Claim and Distribute Rewards

Once delegated, the DeFi protocol’s representative can claim settled rewards using a dedicated on-chain instruction or via SDK/CLI tools. Claimed rewards can then be redistributed to users according to the protocol’s internal emission policy. In brief, this process emulates `fragAsset`\-based reward tracking with **reduced accuracy and flexibility**, tailored for protocols using `wfragAsset`. It is activated and maintained through consensus between Fragmetric governance and the participating DeFi protocol.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#claim-instruction)

Claim Instruction
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can call the `user_claim_reward` instruction of the `restaking program` either on-chain or off-chain. The Anchor IDL is embedded in the [@fragmetric-labs/sdk](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@fragmetric-labs/sdk)
 package. Alternatively, you can download the latest IDL from the [restaking program account](https://explorer.solana.com/address/fragnAis7Bp6FTsMoa6YcH8UffhEw43Ph79qAiK3iF3/anchor-program?cluster=mainnet)
 on Solana Explorer.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/references/defi/reward-distribution#claim-via-sdk)

Claim via SDK
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following CLI session demonstrates reward resolution and claiming.

The CLI and TypeScript SDK interfaces are functionally equivalent. For building an unsigned transaction, you can omit keypairs. Also, for multisig transaction building, you can manually configure the nonce account via the SDK (this is not available via CLI).

Copy

Ask AI

    # Connect with your keypair
    $ pnpx @fragmetric-labs/sdk@latest connect --url devnet --keypairs ./keypairs/wallet.json
    
    # Initialize user context for your wfragAsset token account
    > user = restaking.fragSOL.user('YOUR_WFRAG_ASSET_TOKEN_ACCOUNT_ADDRESS')
    
    # Resolve current reward state
    > user.reward.resolve()
    {
      user: '91zBeWL8kHBaMtaVrHwWsck1UacDKvje82QQ3HE2k8mJ',
      delegate: null,
      receiptTokenMint: 'FRAGSEthVFL7fdqM8hxfxkfCZzUvmg21cqPJVvC1qdbo',
      basePool: {
        contribution: 82_615_701_067_571_732_800n,
        updatedSlot: 380_567_800n,
        tokenAllocatedAmount: {
          totalAmount: 9_280_215_900n,
          records: [ { amount: 9_280_215_900n, contributionAccrualRate: 1 } ]
        },
        settlements: [\
          {\
            reward: {\
              id: 1,\
              name: 'SWTCH',\
              description: 'Switchboard Token',\
              claimable: false,\
              mint: 'FSWSBMV5EB7J8JdafNBLZpfSCLiFwpMCqod2RpkU4RNn',\

Image
-----------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/images#using-markdown)

Using Markdown

The [markdown syntax](https://www.markdownguide.org/basic-syntax/#images)
 lets you add images using the following code

Copy

Ask AI

    ![title](/path/image.jpg)
    

Note that the image file size must be less than 5MB. Otherwise, we recommend hosting on a service like [Cloudinary](https://cloudinary.com/)
 or [S3](https://aws.amazon.com/s3/)
. You can then use that URL and embed.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/images#using-embeds)

Using Embeds

To get more customizability with images, you can also use [embeds](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/writing-content/embed)
 to add images

Copy

Ask AI

    <img height="200" src="/path/image.jpg" />
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/images#embeds-and-html-elements)

Embeds and HTML elements
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  

Mintlify supports [HTML tags in Markdown](https://www.markdownguide.org/basic-syntax/#html)
. This is helpful if you prefer HTML tags to Markdown syntax, and lets you create documentation with infinite flexibility.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/essentials/images#iframes)

iFrames

Loads another HTML page within the document. Most commonly used for embedding videos.

Copy

Ask AI

    <iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/4KzFe50RQkQ"> </iframe>

FRAG-22

Fragmetric’s Core Processes

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#overview)
    
*   [1\. Deposit and Minting](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#1-deposit-and-minting)
    
*   [2\. Reward Tracking and Reward Claim](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#2-reward-tracking-and-reward-claim)
    
*   [3\. Yield Optimization](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#3-yield-optimization)
    
*   [4\. Unstake and Withdraw](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#4-unstake-and-withdraw)
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fragmetric’s FRAG-22 protocol streamlines asset management on Solana through four core processes: Deposit and Minting, Reward Tracking and Claiming, Yield Optimization, and Unstake and Withdraw. Users deposit supported tokens and receive corresponding fragAssets. Rewards are precisely tracked and distributed, and assets are automatically optimized across yield sources. Withdrawals seamlessly redeem underlying assets, ensuring transparency, efficiency, and maximal returns for all participants.

* * *

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#1-deposit-and-minting)

**1\. Deposit and Minting**
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users deposit supported Liquid Staking Tokens (e.g., JitoSOL) into Fragmetric. Fragmetric’s Normalized Token Pool evaluates the deposited asset’s real-time value and mints an equivalent amount of fragAssets (e.g., fragSOL), ensuring accurate asset representation.

*   **Deposit:** User deposits supported assets into the Fragmetric Reserve.
*   **Asset Valuation:** Normalized Token Pool calculates the current value based on integrated pricing sources.
*   **Minting:** Users receive fragAssets proportional to their deposits.

* * *

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#2-reward-tracking-and-reward-claim)

**2\. Reward Tracking and Reward Claim**
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rewards (staking yields, NCN/AVS rewards) are continuously tracked by the FRAG-22 Reward Module. Contributions are calculated dynamically using Solana’s transfer-hook functionality. Users can claim their accrued rewards at any time.

*   **Reward Accumulation:** Rewards accrue proportional to user contributions (balance × time held).
*   **Transfer Tracking:** Contribution recalculates upon any token transfer (transfer-hook).
*   **Claiming Rewards:** Users initiate claims, and rewards transfer from the Reward Reserve.

* * *

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#3-yield-optimization)

**3\. Yield Optimization**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fragmetric automatically optimizes yields by strategically allocating deposited assets across yield sources (such as restaking protocols for NCN/AVS networks). Yield Source Adapters regularly harvest these yields, ensuring optimized returns.

*   **Allocation:** Assets automatically allocated to highest-yielding sources.
*   **Yield Generation:** Assets accrue additional yield through external protocols (NCN/AVS).
*   **Yield Harvesting:** Periodically collected and stored in the Reward Pool.

* * *

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric#4-unstake-and-withdraw)

**4\. Unstake and Withdraw**
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Upon withdrawal request, Fragmetric processes unstaking via the Normalized Token Pool. fragAssets are burned proportionally, redeeming underlying assets back to users based on current valuations.

*   **Withdrawal Request:** User initiates unstake and withdrawal.
*   **Burn Tokens:** fragAssets burned to redeem underlying assets.
*   **Asset Redemption:** Underlying assets proportionally released to the user.

[Overview](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Overview](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/fund/overview)

FRAG-22

*   [Technical Innovation of FRAG-22](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#technical-innovation-of-frag-22)
    
*   [Future, brought to you by FRAG-22](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#future%2C-brought-to-you-by-frag-22)
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#frag-22)

FRAG-22
---------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#fragmetric-asset-standard)

Fragmetric Asset Standard

The **FRAG-22 standard** represents an advanced asset tokenization framework developed by Fragmetric, built upon Solana’s innovative Token 2022 - **transfer hook**. Initially utilized for liquid restaking, the standard now provides robust capabilities to support multiple asset deposits, diverse reward distributions, and seamless adoption of various yield-generating strategies beyond traditional staking solutions.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#expansion-beyond-restaking)

**Expansion Beyond Restaking**

Fragmetric initially introduced the **FRAG-22** standard to support its Liquid Restaking Tokens, allowing multiple LSTs to be deposited, automatically generating and accurately distributing multiple reward streams created by NCNs. With this robust and modular infrastructure, restaking served as the first use case demonstrating the standard’s potential. Recognizing broader opportunities, Fragmetric expanded the standard’s applicability beyond restaking, integrating diverse yield generation methods into a unified, composable token architecture. This expansion enables FRAG-22 assets to seamlessly integrate with liquidity pools, lending protocols, structured DeFi products, and more complex yield-generation strategies.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#technical-innovation-of-frag-22)

Technical Innovation of FRAG-22
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unified Multi-Asset Deposits

FRAG-22 introduces an advanced multi-asset capability, enabling the simultaneous deposit of diverse tokens under one unified standard. Through sophisticated normalization and token aggregation protocols, this functionality simplifies complex multi-asset management tasks. By standardizing diverse asset classes into a singular, fungible token, FRAG-22 significantly enhances liquidity efficiency and reduces transaction overhead, enabling streamlined implementation of complex yield strategies without additional user friction.

Precision Real-Time Multi-Reward Distribution

Built on top of Solana’s innovative token 2022 - transfer hook, FRAG-22 delivers unprecedented precision in the tracking and calculation of multiple reward streams. Every transaction triggers real-time, on-chain recalculations, ensuring accurate, up-to-date reward allocations even under high-frequency trading conditions. Users retain explicit control, manually claiming accumulated rewards via Fragmetric’s decentralized application interface, fostering full transparency and fairness, particularly valuable in environments with complex transactional interactions.

Modular Yield Integration Framework

FRAG-22 is architected with a highly modular design, facilitating rapid integration and adoption of diverse yield sources. This framework supports a plug-and-play model for incorporating liquidity pools, lending platforms, structured financial products, yield farms, and emerging decentralized finance strategies. The protocol’s adaptable architecture ensures quick scalability and continuous expansion of yield opportunities, allowing Fragmetric to dynamically respond to market innovations and user demands, consistently optimizing user returns and capital efficiency.

> We believe that the FRAG-22 standard will unlock innovative token use cases within the Solana ecosystem by enabling seamless adoption of diverse decentralized yield sources, including but not limited to restaking services.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview#future%2C-brought-to-you-by-frag-22)

**Future, brought to you by FRAG-22**
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By seamlessly integrating multi-asset deposits, precise reward distribution, and modular yield sourcing, Fragmetric’s FRAG-22 standard unlocks the next generation of decentralized finance. It empowers developers and users alike with streamlined access to sophisticated DeFi strategies, superior liquidity management, and transparent reward tracking-setting a new benchmark for composability, scalability, and user experience on Solana. **STAKE TWICE, EARN MORE**

[Fragmetric’s Core Processes](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/fragmetric)

Wrap & Unwrap (DeFi Mode)

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [wfragSOL & wfragJTO](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#wfragsol-%26-wfragjto)
    
*   [What are wfragSol & wfragJTO](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#what-are-wfragsol-%26-wfragjto)
    
*   [How to wrap and unwrap](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#how-to-wrap-and-unwrap)
    

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#wfragsol-%26-wfragjto)

wfragSOL & wfragJTO
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

fragSOL and fragJTO utilize the Transfer Hook of Token Extension (also known as Token-2022), an advanced token program on the Solana blockchain. While Token-2022 is becoming increasingly common in DeFi recently, many dApps still do not support it. To integrate with such dApps, there’s another form of Fragmetric Restaked Tokens called wfragSOL (Wrapped Fragmetric Restaked SOL), wfragJTO (Wrapped Fragmetric Restaked JTO).

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#what-are-wfragsol-%26-wfragjto)

What are wfragSol & wfragJTO
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

wfragSOL and wfragJTO are standard SPL tokens that represent an account’s share of the total supply of fragSOL and fragJTO, respectively. They serve as the wrapped versions of fragSOL and fragJTO, designed to maximize DeFi compatibility. For example, when converting fragSOL to wfragSOL, the corresponding amount of fragSOL is locked in the wfragSOL program’s token account, and an equal amount of wfragSOL is minted. Conversely, when unwrapping wfragSOL, it is burned, and the equivalent amount of fragSOL is unlocked. wfragSOL holders can always convert wfragSOL to fragSOL at a 1:1 ratio, and vice versa.

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/wrap-unwrap#how-to-wrap-and-unwrap)

How to wrap and unwrap
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Step to Wrap & Unwrap\
---------------------\
\
Maximize the DeFi utility of your fragAsset via wrapping](https://fragmetriclabs.mintlify.app/Documentation/Guides/Wrap-Unwrap)

Normalized Token Pool

Overview

[Documentation](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/home/get-started/welcome)
[Fragmetric Protocol](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/overview)
[Assets](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/assets/fragsol)
[Developers](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/dev/solana-programs)

On this page

*   [Key Functionalities:](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/ntp/overview#key-functionalities%3A)
    

The **Normalized Token Pool** within the FRAG-22 ecosystem serves as an essential mechanism for efficiently handling multiple asset types in a unified, composable manner. By standardizing different types of deposited tokens into a single, fungible token representation, it significantly simplifies asset management, enhances liquidity efficiency, and optimizes capital utilization across the protocol. At its core, the Normalized Token Pool aggregates diverse underlying assets deposited by users, assigning normalized values to maintain fair proportionality. This approach ensures seamless integration with various yield strategies, liquidity provisions, and DeFi applications, effectively removing complexity from multi-asset management.

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/ntp/overview#key-functionalities%3A)

**Key Functionalities:**

*   **Asset Normalization:** Translates deposited assets into a common token representation, ensuring consistency in valuation and reward calculation.
*   **Liquidity Optimization:** Pools normalized assets to maximize efficiency, enabling simpler and faster reallocation of assets to yield-generating sources.
*   **Simplified Asset Management:** Reduces operational overhead for users and developers by abstracting away complexities associated with handling multiple distinct asset types.
*   **Composability and Interoperability:** Facilitates effortless integration with external DeFi applications, enabling users to leverage their normalized asset positions across diverse financial protocols seamlessly.

The Normalized Token Pool thus forms a robust foundation within FRAG-22, enabling highly efficient, scalable, and simplified asset interactions across decentralized finance.

[Yield Source Adapters](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/yield-source/adapter)
[Normalized Token](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/ntp/normalized-token)

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.fragmetric.xyz/protocol/module/fund/overview#overview)

**Overview**

The Fund module serves as the core liquidity management, and accounting engine within the FRAG-22 ecosystem. It securely manages user deposits and withdrawals, maintains precise onchain records, and ensures liquidity efficiency. By providing robust fund management and transparent accounting, it lays the foundation for secure and efficient decentralized asset management.
